; Function Attrs: nounwind ssp uwtable
define i32 @mbedtls_mpi_add_int(%struct.mbedtls_mpi* %X, %struct.mbedtls_mpi* %A, i64 %b) #0 {
entry:
  %_B = alloca %struct.mbedtls_mpi, align 8

  call void @llvm.dbg.value(metadata i64 %b, i64 0, metadata !1086, metadata !264), !dbg !1087
  call void @llvm.dbg.declare(metadata %struct.mbedtls_mpi* %_B, metadata !1088, metadata !264), !dbg !1089
  call void @llvm.dbg.declare(metadata [1 x i64]* %p, metadata !1090, metadata !264), !dbg !1091
  %cmp = icmp slt i64 %b, 0, !dbg !1092

cond.true:                                        ; preds = %entry

  br label %cond.end, !dbg !1093

cond.false:                                       ; preds = %entry

  %cond = phi i64 [ %sub, %cond.true ], [ %b, %cond.false ], !dbg !1093

  %cmp1 = icmp slt i64 %b, 0, !dbg !1097
  %cond2 = select i1 %cmp1, i32 -1, i32 1, !dbg !1098
  %s = getelementptr inbounds %struct.mbedtls_mpi, %struct.mbedtls_mpi* %_B, i32 0, i32 0, !dbg !1099
  store i32 %cond2, i32* %s, align 4, !dbg !1100
  %n = getelementptr inbounds %struct.mbedtls_mpi, %struct.mbedtls_mpi* %_B, i32 0, i32 1, !dbg !1101
  store i64 1, i64* %n, align 8, !dbg !1102
  %arraydecay = getelementptr inbounds [1 x i64], [1 x i64]* %p, i32 0, i32 0, !dbg !1103

; Function Attrs: nounwind ssp uwtable
define internal void @mpi_montg_init(i64* %mm, %struct.mbedtls_mpi* %N) #0 {

  %and = and i64 %add, 4, !dbg !3250

  %add1 = add i64 %1, %shl, !dbg !3252

  call void @llvm.dbg.value(metadata i32 64, i64 0, metadata !3253, metadata !264), !dbg !3255
  br label %for.cond, !dbg !3256

for.cond:                                         ; preds = %for.inc, %entry
  %x.0 = phi i64 [ %add1, %entry ], [ %mul2, %for.inc ]
  %i.0 = phi i32 [ 64, %entry ], [ %div, %for.inc ]

; Function Attrs: nounwind ssp uwtable

; Function Attrs: nounwind ssp uwtable
define i32 @mbedtls_mpi_is_prime(%struct.mbedtls_mpi* %X, i32 (i8*, i8*, i64)* %f_rng, i8* %p_rng) #0 {
entry:
  %XX = alloca %struct.mbedtls_mpi, align 8

  %s = getelementptr inbounds %struct.mbedtls_mpi, %struct.mbedtls_mpi* %XX, i32 0, i32 0, !dbg !3783
  store i32 1, i32* %s, align 4, !dbg !3784

  %0 = load i64, i64* %n, align 8, !dbg !3785

  store i64 %0, i64* %n1, align 8, !dbg !3787
  %p = getelementptr inbounds %struct.mbedtls_mpi, %struct.mbedtls_mpi* %X, i32 0, i32 2, !dbg !3788
  %1 = load i64*, i64** %p, align 8, !dbg !3788
  %p2 = getelementptr inbounds %struct.mbedtls_mpi, %struct.mbedtls_mpi* %XX, i32 0, i32 2, !dbg !3789
  store i64* %1, i64** %p2, align 8, !dbg !3790
  %call = call i32 @mbedtls_mpi_cmp_int(%struct.mbedtls_mpi* %XX, i64 0), !dbg !3791
  %cmp = icmp eq i32 %call, 0, !dbg !3793
  br i1 %cmp, label %if.then, label %lor.lhs.false, !dbg !3794

lor.lhs.false:                                    ; preds = %entry
  %call3 = call i32 @mbedtls_mpi_cmp_int(%struct.mbedtls_mpi* %XX, i64 1), !dbg !3795
  %cmp4 = icmp eq i32 %call3, 0, !dbg !3796
  br i1 %cmp4, label %if.then, label %if.end, !dbg !3797

if.then:                                          ; preds = %lor.lhs.false, %entry
  br label %return, !dbg !3798

if.end:                                           ; preds = %lor.lhs.false
  %call5 = call i32 @mbedtls_mpi_cmp_int(%struct.mbedtls_mpi* %XX, i64 2), !dbg !3799
  %cmp6 = icmp eq i32 %call5, 0, !dbg !3801
  br i1 %cmp6, label %if.then7, label %if.end8, !dbg !3802

if.then7:                                         ; preds = %if.end
  br label %return, !dbg !3803

if.end8:                                          ; preds = %if.end
  %call9 = call i32 @mpi_check_small_factors(%struct.mbedtls_mpi* %XX), !dbg !3804
  call void @llvm.dbg.value(metadata i32 %call9, i64 0, metadata !3806, metadata !264), !dbg !3807
  %cmp10 = icmp ne i32 %call9, 0, !dbg !3808
  br i1 %cmp10, label %if.then11, label %if.end15, !dbg !3809

if.then11:                                        ; preds = %if.end8

  br label %return, !dbg !3814

return:                                           ; preds = %if.end15, %if.end14, %if.then13, %if.then7, %if.then
  %retval.0 = phi i32 [ -14, %if.then ], [ 0, %if.then7 ], [ 0, %if.then13 ], [ %call9, %if.end14 ], [ %call16, %if.end15 ]

; Function Attrs: nounwind ssp uwtable
define internal i32 @mpi_check_small_factors(%struct.mbedtls_mpi* %X) #0 {
entry:
  %r = alloca i64, align 8
  call void @llvm.dbg.value(metadata %struct.mbedtls_mpi* %X, i64 0, metadata !3819, metadata !264), !dbg !3820
  call void @llvm.dbg.value(metadata i32 0, i64 0, metadata !3821, metadata !264), !dbg !3822
  call void @llvm.dbg.declare(metadata i64* %r, metadata !3823, metadata !264), !dbg !3824
  %p = getelementptr inbounds %struct.mbedtls_mpi, %struct.mbedtls_mpi* %X, i32 0, i32 2, !dbg !3825
  %0 = load i64*, i64** %p, align 8, !dbg !3825
  %arrayidx = getelementptr inbounds i64, i64* %0, i64 0, !dbg !3827
  %1 = load i64, i64* %arrayidx, align 8, !dbg !3827
  %and = and i64 %1, 1, !dbg !3828
  %cmp = icmp eq i64 %and, 0, !dbg !3829
  br i1 %cmp, label %if.then, label %if.end, !dbg !3830

if.then:                                          ; preds = %entry
  br label %return, !dbg !3831

if.end:                                           ; preds = %entry
  call void @llvm.dbg.value(metadata i64 0, i64 0, metadata !3832, metadata !264), !dbg !3833
  br label %for.cond, !dbg !3834

  %ret.0 = phi i32 [ 0, %if.end ], [ %call10, %for.inc ]

if.end182:                                        ; preds = %if.then180, %for.end
  br label %cleanup, !dbg !4384

cleanup:                                          ; preds = %if.end182, %if.end176, %if.then161, %if.then154, %if.then143, %if.end127, %if.then114, %if.then108, %if.end99, %if.then86, %if.then80, %if.end71, %if.then56, %if.then50, %if.then44, %if.end35, %if.then22, %if.then16, %if.then10, %if.then4, %if.then
  %ret.1 = phi i32 [ %call, %if.then ], [ %call2, %if.then4 ], [ %call8, %if.then10 ], [ %call14, %if.then16 ], [ %call20, %if.then22 ], [ 1, %if.end35 ], [ %call42, %if.then44 ], [ %call48, %if.then50 ], [ %call54, %if.then56 ], [ 1, %if.end71 ], [ %call78, %if.then80 ], [ %call84, %if.then86 ], [ 1, %if.end99 ], [ %call106, %if.then108 ], [ %call112, %if.then114 ], [ 1, %if.end127 ], [ %call140, %if.then143 ], [ %call151, %if.then154 ], [ %call158, %if.then161 ], [ 1, %if.end176 ], [ %ret.0, %if.end182 ]
  %cmp183 = icmp ne i32 %ret.1, 0, !dbg !4385
  br i1 %cmp183, label %land.lhs.true, label %if.end189, !dbg !4387

land.lhs.true:                                    ; preds = %cleanup
  %cmp185 = icmp ne i32 %verbose, 0, !dbg !4388
  br i1 %cmp185, label %if.then187, label %if.end189, !dbg !4389

if.then187:                                       ; preds = %land.lhs.true
  %call188 = call i32 (i8*, ...) @printf(i8* getelementptr inbounds ([38 x i8], [38 x i8]* @.str20, i32 0, i32 0), i32 %ret.1), !dbg !4390
  br label %if.end189, !dbg !4390

if.end189:                                        ; preds = %if.then187, %land.lhs.true, %cleanup
  call void @mbedtls_mpi_free(%struct.mbedtls_mpi* %A), !dbg !4391
  call void @mbedtls_mpi_free(%struct.mbedtls_mpi* %E), !dbg !4392
  call void @mbedtls_mpi_free(%struct.mbedtls_mpi* %N), !dbg !4393
  call void @mbedtls_mpi_free(%struct.mbedtls_mpi* %X), !dbg !4394
  call void @mbedtls_mpi_free(%struct.mbedtls_mpi* %Y), !dbg !4395
  call void @mbedtls_mpi_free(%struct.mbedtls_mpi* %U), !dbg !4396
  call void @mbedtls_mpi_free(%struct.mbedtls_mpi* %V), !dbg !4397
  %cmp190 = icmp ne i32 %verbose, 0, !dbg !4398
  br i1 %cmp190, label %if.then192, label %if.end194, !dbg !4400

if.then192:                                       ; preds = %if.end189
  %call193 = call i32 (i8*, ...) @printf(i8* getelementptr inbounds ([2 x i8], [2 x i8]* @.str21, i32 0, i32 0)), !dbg !4401
  br label %if.end194, !dbg !4401

if.end194:                                        ; preds = %if.then192, %if.end189
  ret i32 %ret.1, !dbg !4402
}
